 restmas clease nilsanham aise daur main hai jab soochnaaon kaa pravaah abaadh he or mobile internet kii pahunch main vruddhi main visphot se adhik se adhik bharatiyon tak jis raftaar se suchanaaen pahunch rahi hai, vaisaa itihaas main kabhi nahin rahaa
 With more than two billion websites, search engines, social media and billions of people using messaging applications and billions of videos available on video sharing websites, Indians living online have access to so much and diverse information that digital It was not imaginable even before the era
 samasya yah he ki is soochna kaa bada hissaa bakawaas he, uskaa kuch hissaa to vyaktiyon or samaaj, donon ke liye ghaatak he or bakawaas ke is samudr main soochnaaon ke dwipon tak pahunchane ke liye ham jin plateformon par bharosa karte hai, unhen har taah ke durupyog se bachaane ke liye sangharsh karnaa padataa he or kai baar to lagata he ki ve na keval samasyamoolak saamagree or vyavhaar ko sahaara de rahe hai, balki uskaa vistaar bhi kar rahe hai
 Such a situation is better in terms of access to information to millions of Indians, but with this it makes them helpless in front of all kinds of new threats
 ye khatre kai baar to jane-pahachaane or puraane hai, jaise phayda paane ke laalchee, rajnatik shaktiyaan yaa kuch sankeern maansikta vaale log, jo dusron par apni kalpit shreshthata jamaane ke prayaas se milane vaale santosh kii khatir sakriy rahete hai yaa phir aise khatre hote hai jo digital media takanic ke kaam karne ke tareekon se yaa sambandhit plateform ke nepathy main sakriy vyavsaayon athwa in upkarnon evam pranaaliyon ke istemaal ke tareeke se badhate hai
 What are the problems? For many of the information available online, 'rubbish' is a good word, but if someone wants to understand the issues of our times properly, then there are many differences
 isse adhik saaf paribhaasha cleyar wardley or hossain darakhshaan lekar aae hai, jo 'farji soochna' (juthi lekin jaan-boojhkar na daali gai ho), 'dushprachaar' (jaan-boojhkar galat soochna failaana) or 'kusuchana' (aisi soochna jo puri yaa aanshik taur par sachhee ho sakati he lekin kisi ko nuksaan pahunchane kii niyat se failaai jaati he) ke rup main he
 These different types of problematic materials are formulated and propagated from different circles for different purposes
 farji soochna, dushprachaar or kusuchana phaayde ke liye kai baar nae halkon or kai baar to sthapit media kii ore se bhi prasaarit kii jaati he, jo behad dukhad he
 (asking what is 'fake news'?) Many people will point to poor journalism or corrupt or greed-driven editorial methods when asked
 )in sabhi shreniyon kii suchanaaen rajnatik netaa or unke samarthak satta hasil karne ke liye karte hai
 (for example, a government can also refuse major protests, even if reliable news media publishes footage to prove it wrong
 ) ant main, sabase jatil baat yah he ki log khud-ba-khud kabhi-kabhaar farji soochna, dushprachaar or kusuchana ko sahi maanakar aage badha dete hai
 (there is no scientific evidence that any type of urine can cure cancer of humans or other mammal animals, but some people continue to promote such claims, and usually with all faith and seriousness
 )in sabake alaava or bhi samasyaayein hai jinka sambandh soochna kii sachaai se nahin, balki uski vyakhya ke syah paksh par jor dene kii style se sambandhit he
 For example, when some of us, sometimes very active, sometimes on a large scale and sometimes together, target someone about his race, religion, sex, caste, etc
 iskaa sabase kurup cheharaa to nafrat failaane vaale bhaashanon or sahitya main dikhataa he, jo hinsa bhadakaate hai jiskaa parinaam kai baar khooni sangharshon ke rup main saamne aata he
 Old problems, new problems are all old problems
 kabhi-kabhi kuch prakaashak logon ko gumraah karte hai, kabhi kuch taqatvar netaa jhooth bolte hai or use prachaarit karte hai, kabhi-kabhi hamamen se kuch log jaan-boojhkar yaa anjaane main juthi or bhraamak chizon ko aage badhaate hai
 And, we do not often have mutual coherence, and sometimes we actively try to degrade, humiliate or embarrass each other
 lekin yahaan nai chijen bhi hai jinka sambandh is baat se he ki ham apane liye praasangik jaankaree ke dwipon kii khoj main online bakawaas ke mahaasaagar main kaise or kin raaston se hokar guzarate hai
 a recent survey of English-language Internet users in India with my colleagues can better explain this issue
 purv-digital daur main, ham saarvajanik maamalon par jaankaree ke liye aam taur par sidhe akhbaar-patrikaon or radio-tivi kii ore rukh karte the
 But this is not the case in online rounds
 hamaare surveykshan main bhartiya logon main se keval 18 pratishat ne hi kaha ki ve online samachar khojane ke mukhya tareeke ke rup main sidhe akhbaar-patrikaon yaa radio-tivi kii websiton yaa ap par jate hai
 In contrast, 32 per cent said that they trust search engines and 24 per cent believed on social media
 iskaa matlab yah hua ki google or fasebuk jaisi companiyaan soochnaaon or khabaron ke maamle main aaj bharat ke kisi bhi sampadak kii tulana main adhik mahatvapurn online dwarpal hai
 This situation is very different from the pre-digital world
 yah shodh is baat kaa dastavej he ki kaise search ingine or soshal media, donon aam taur par logon ko unki talash kii apeksha duusare samaacharon kii ore le jate hai, or is baat kaa bhi dastavej he ki log hameshaa yah nahin jaanate hai ki unhen samachar dene vaale koun hai, jiske kaaran ve dushprachaar failaane waalon kaa shikaar ban kar kuch bhi clic karte hi uske strot kii pahchaan kiye yaa uski vishwasaneeyata or uske peeche ke iraadon ko jane bina hi usase prabhavit ho uthte hai
 New problems do not end here
 digital media or plateform pradaan karne vaali companiyon kii sankhya main badhotaree ne keval suchanaaen praapt karne ke hamaare tareekon ko hi nahin badal diya he, balki hamaare unase judye yaa unka upyog karne ke tareekon main bhi badlaav kiya he
 Indians have shown an urge to interact and participate actively in social media and messaging platforms, and a large number of people in our survey reported that they share news on platforms such as Facebook and whatsapp and contemporary issues from friends and strangers Use them to discuss
 yah sab zyaadaatar bina kisi durbhaavna ke (yaa kuch maamalon main yun hi bina kuch soche-vichaare) hota he
 It is a great thing that people can not only get information but can also discuss them with others
 asli samasya yah he ki ye plateform hamen soochnaaon tak pahunch or un par charchaa kaa behad aasaan mauka dete hai, unase dusron ko tang karne ke aasaan tareeke bhi mil jate hai, jo kabhi-kabhi rajnatik dalon ke khaas makasad se karte hai
 This creates a huge problem especially in divided societies and polarized political environment
 bhartiya logon ko is baat kaa katai andaja nahin he ki ve is nae or badalte hue media vaataavaran main kitne majaboor hai

 yah ashanka or sanshay rajnatik dabaav ke aage ekadam sharnaagat media or 'ped news' kii anek ghatnaon ke maddenjar jaij hi kaha jayega

 Apart from this, the problem is that the platforms that we rely on to reach the right places on the Internet, many times companies start targeting people and promoting propaganda
 aise main is sabase bachakar kaise internet kaa sarvaadhik laabh uthaaya ja saktaa he?inamen kuch chunautiyaan to behad puraani or hameshaa hi maujuud rahi hai, khaskar vividh saanskrithik or bante hue samaajon main hamaare jivan kaa avibhajya ang hai, jinamein ham aksar sahi or galat par aapas main sahamat nahin hote or jahaan ek vyakti ke liye mahatvapurn soochna ko doosraa vyakti bakawaas yaa khatarnaak bhi maan saktaa he
 We will probably never be monopolized on these issues
 haalanki, kuch chunautiyaan nai hai or ye kisi or baat se zyada isse sambandh rakhti hai ki pramukh plateform pradaata companiyaan swatantra abhivyakti kii adhisanrachana ke bade hisse par niyantran or laabh ke liye uskaa sanchaalan karne ke saath paidaa hone vaale uttardayitvon kaa nirvaah kaise karti hai
 Globally, and also in India, our prospects have just begun
 kaarobaar or maanavadhikaron ke sambandh main sanyukt raashtra ke maardarshak siddhant is disha main prasthaan bindu jaise hai
 Accordingly, it is the responsibility of the companies providing the platform of communication to protect our fundamental right to free expression, which is not limited only to the 'right' statement, but also to shocking, hurting and disturbing others
 
 lekin saath hi saath logon ko kshati se—khaas taur par ghrinaaspad or hinsa bhadakaane yaa uksaane vaale vaktavyon se—bachaane kii karrwai bhi karen

 swatantra nigaraanee kii or logon ke liye behatar maahaul kaayam karne ke liye jarurat is baat kii he ki plateform pradaan karne vaali companiyaan spasht or bodhgamy maahaul uplabdh karaaen, jisamen log apane bharose ke madhyam kaa chunaav kar saken or samast data tisare pakshon ko uplabdh ho taaki ve utpaadon or sevaaon ke kaam karne ke tareekon or upyogon kii jaanch kar saken

 In the 18th century, India had given to Brazil, you may have heard about the lion of Gir forest in Gujarat, but less information about the cows of Gir
 Only people have it
 gir kii gaayen bharat kii aam gaayon ke mukaable doguna doodh detii hai
 The Gir cow can give milk up to a maximum of 5 thousand liters after giving birth to a baby, while a normal cow can give milk from 2 to 2
5 thousand liters

 In recent years, the number of cows of indigenous breed has decreased in India
 pashu vigyaniyon ke alaava centre sarkaar ne is par chintaa jataai thi

 *** pakistan ke purv army chif general raahil sharif ko saudi arab ke netritv main bani 39 deshon kii islamic sainya gathbandhan kii kaman die jane par iran ne nakhushi jataai he
 Iran has expressed its concern that it is not 'satisfied' with this alliance
 pakistan main iran ke rajdoot mehandi hunardost ne iran kii sarkari news agency IRNA kaha ki pakistan ne raahil sharif ko gathbandhan sena kaa netritv karne ke liye anaapatti pramaan patr (no abjection certificate) jari karne se pehle iran ke adhikariyon se sampark kiya tha
 According to the report of Pakistani newspaper 'dawn', Hunardost said, "but this does not mean that Iran is satisfied with this decision or has accepted it
" ' tehran ne islamabad ko bataa diya he ki iran aise kisi sainya gathbandhan kaa hissaa nahin banegaa
 Hunardost also said that Iran has never expressed a desire to be part of such an alliance
 mehandi hunardost ne suzav diya he ki sabhi muslim desh is tarah ke vivaadit sainya gathbandhan banane ke bajaay apane vivaad ko sulajhane ke liye ek saath milakar 'shanti gathbandhan' bananaa chahie
 Significantly, in 2015, Saudi Arabia announced an alliance with 34 Muslim country's forces to fight terrorism
 pakistan bhi is gathbandhan kaa sadsy bana tha
 On Saturday, Hunardosta gave an interview to the Pakistani newspaper Express Tribune when asked if Iran would be part of this Islamic military alliance
 hunardost ne kaha ki iran gathbandhan main shaamil hone kii apni ichha ko pehle hi bataa chukaa he

 saudi arab or uske padosi desh lagaataar kai maheenon se yaman main iran samarthit vidrohiyon se jang lard rahe hai, or vahaan saikadon hawaii hamale kar chuke hai
